The operator can place a calibrated specimen in the cell of the Point Load Testing System for calibration of the crosshead position. The application uses a two-point calibration for the crosshead position.\r\n\r\nUsing this application, specimen measurements can be made with ease. This App can be used with diametral, axial, or irregular specimens. In addition, the application can be set to reuse certain dimensions, so if a core sample is used, the application can be set to use the same diameter for each specimen tested.\r\n\r\nThe operator can also define a custom equation for determination of the unconfined compressive strength from the point load strength index as calculated by the test.
